<h1 class="kt-adv-heading2_ddb205-bb script wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2_ddb205-bb">Slow Travel &amp; Digital Nomad Life</h1>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-b58af18568d1eef555dfd2f52cbf9fee" style="padding-right:0;padding-left:0;font-size:20px">Your go-to guide for budget-friendly and meaningful travel experiences off the beaten path.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id2_20d40c-26 alignfull has-theme-palette6-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-row kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_19ae45-5c kb-section-dir-vertical kb-section-md-dir-vertical kb-section-sm-dir-vertical"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_0b51b0-9c kb-section-dir-vertical rotate90"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"></div></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_c049f7-60"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading2_9683c9-a4 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2_9683c9-a4">Hi! We&#8217;re Allan &amp; Katharina</h2>



<p>But you can call us All &amp; Kat! For over 6 years, we have been slow-traveling the world full-time as digital nomads, staying in 20+ countries and choosing local experiences over tourist hotspots.</p>



<p>Our mission is to inspire <strong>budget-friendly and off the beaten path adventures</strong> that leave a positive impact on you and your surroundings. That’s why you’ll find us in homestays or at a street food cart rather than a fancy rooftop bar. 🌮</p>



<p>On <em>Nomads Beyond</em>, we go beyond typical tourist spots &#8211; we dive deep into local life and seek meaningful travel experiences while working online and living intentionally.</p>



<p>Whether you’re looking for offbeat destinations, mindful travel guides or practical tips on how to become a slow traveler or digital nomad too – this is your resource to make it happen!</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns2_46e103-60"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn2_865cec-61 kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-inherit  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-button__link wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://nomadsbeyond.com/about/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">More about us</span></a></div>
</div></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<h2 class="kt-adv-heading2_0fb3ce-33 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2_0fb3ce-33">Start Here</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading2_afa985-d2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2_afa985-d2">Browse our destinations guides, digital nomad tips and resources to inspire and plan your own slow travel adventure.</p>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2_deae3f-64"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading2_ed86f9-e9 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2_ed86f9-e9">What is Slow Travel?</h2>



<p>Funny enough we started off as fast travelers &#8211; seeing as many places and sights as we could in a short amount of time. While this is exciting it’s also really draining for your body, mind and wallet.</p>



<p>When we started to adapt a slower pace we were able to <strong>truly immerse ourselves</strong> into the culture, nature, food and people around us. Which is so much more rewarding! 😌</p>



<p>Traveling slow also helps us to cut down costs immensely so we can travel full-time. That&#8217;s why we often stay weeks or months in one place and soak it all in.</p>



<p>Do you want to travel deeper and longer too? Check out our slow travel resources to get started!</p>

</div></div>
